### [335] [Combining Cost-Constrained Runtime Monitors for AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15886)
*Tim Tian Hua,James Baskerville,Henri Lemoine,Mia Hopman,Aryan Bhatt,Tyler Tracy*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种结合多个运行时监视器的协议，以在成本受限的情况下最大化检测错误输出的概率，并在代码审查任务中取得了显著的改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究如何将多个运行时监视器组合成单个监视协议，以在满足平均情况预算约束的同时，最大限度地提高对错误输出应用安全干预措施的概率（即最大化召回率）。

Method: 通过穷举搜索研究了何时以及调用哪些监视器，并根据 Neyman-Pearson 引理分配安全干预措施。

Result: 在代码审查环境中，与朴素基线相比，召回率提高了一倍以上；并证明了结合两个监视器可以比单独使用任何一个监视器产生更优的帕累托效果。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种原则性的方法，用于在成本敏感的环境中结合现有监视器来检测不良行为。

Abstract: Monitoring AIs at runtime can help us detect and stop harmful actions. In
this paper, we study how to combine multiple runtime monitors into a single
monitoring protocol. The protocol's objective is to maximize the probability of
applying a safety intervention on misaligned outputs (i.e., maximize recall).
Since running monitors and applying safety interventions are costly, the
protocol also needs to adhere to an average-case budget constraint. Taking the
monitors' performance and cost as given, we develop an algorithm to find the
most efficient protocol. The algorithm exhaustively searches over when and
which monitors to call, and allocates safety interventions based on the
Neyman-Pearson lemma. By focusing on likelihood ratios and strategically
trading off spending on monitors against spending on interventions, we more
than double our recall rate compared to a naive baseline in a code review
setting. We also show that combining two monitors can Pareto dominate using
either monitor alone. Our framework provides a principled methodology for
combining existing monitors to detect undesirable behavior in cost-sensitive
settings.

</details>


### [336] [Verifying International Agreements on AI: Six Layers of Verification for Rules on Large-Scale AI Development and Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15916)
*Mauricio Baker,Gabriel Kulp,Oliver Marks,Miles Brundage,Lennart Heim*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 前沿AI的风险需要国际合作和验证。本报告概述了AI验证的方法、挑战和所需研究。可行的验证方法包括芯片安全功能、监控设备和举报人计划。然而，这些方法仍需开发和测试，并需要监管以防滥用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本报告旨在为政策专业人士和技术研究人员提供AI验证的深入概述，以期为AI安全和国际合作提供更清晰、更详细的指导。

Method: 该研究通过梳理现有文献、专家访谈和原创分析，为AI验证提供了概念框架、实施选项和研发挑战的概述。

Result: 该研究发现，国家可以通过六种基本独立但具有冗余性的验证方法来核实合规性：AI芯片内置安全功能、连接到AI芯片的独立监控设备，以及基于人员的机制（如举报人计划）。

Conclusion: 该研究提出，人工智能（AI）验证对于国际合作至关重要，尤其是在应对前沿AI的风险方面。虽然存在多种验证方法，但许多技术仍需开发和测试，并且需要明确的监管措施来防止滥用和权力集中。为了实现对大规模AI开发和部署的合规性验证，必须在研究与开发方面取得重大进展。

Abstract: The risks of frontier AI may require international cooperation, which in turn
may require verification: checking that all parties follow agreed-on rules. For
instance, states might need to verify that powerful AI models are widely
deployed only after their risks to international security have been evaluated
and deemed manageable. However, research on AI verification could benefit from
greater clarity and detail. To address this, this report provides an in-depth
overview of AI verification, intended for both policy professionals and
technical researchers. We present novel conceptual frameworks, detailed
implementation options, and key R&D challenges. These draw on existing
literature, expert interviews, and original analysis, all within the scope of
confidentially overseeing AI development and deployment that uses thousands of
high-end AI chips. We find that states could eventually verify compliance by
using six largely independent verification approaches with substantial
redundancy: (1) built-in security features in AI chips; (2-3) separate
monitoring devices attached to AI chips; and (4-6) personnel-based mechanisms,
such as whistleblower programs. While promising, these approaches require
guardrails to protect against abuse and power concentration, and many of these
technologies have yet to be built or stress-tested. To enable states to
confidently verify compliance with rules on large-scale AI development and
deployment, the R&D challenges we list need significant progress.

</details>


### [337] [Chameleon Channels: Measuring YouTube Accounts Repurposed for Deception and Profit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16045)
*Alejandro Cuevas,Manoel Horta Ribeiro,Nicolas Christin*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 在线内容创作者会改变频道内容和身份，这在 YouTube 上很常见，被转售的频道中有37%传播有害内容，即使订阅者增加。这种行为利用了用户对频道的信任，并且可能随着市场增长而加剧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在线内容创作者在改变频道内容和身份时，利用已有用户群的现象，以及这种行为在 YouTube 等平台上的普遍性。

Method: 通过观察和分析在6个月内转售的 YouTube 频道（其中37%被用于传播潜在有害内容，订阅者不减反增）以及收集两个时间点的140万个 YouTube 频道信息（估计有0.25%的频道被重新使用，这些频道通常包含潜在问题内容，例如成为虚假信息频道或链接到金融诈骗网页），来研究频道内容被篡改的问题。

Result: 研究发现，约37%的二手频道被用来传播潜在有害内容，并且订阅者似乎不减反增。在更广泛的范围内，估计有0.25%的频道在三个月内被重新使用，这些频道包含潜在问题内容，如虚假信息和金融诈骗。

Conclusion: 该现象不仅限于 YouTube，并且如果继续不受技术或其它形式的缓解措施的挑战，那么精心培养的有机受众市场将会增长。

Abstract: Online content creators spend significant time and effort building their user
base through a long, often arduous process, which requires finding the right
``niche'' to cater to. So, what incentive is there for an established content
creator known for cat memes to completely reinvent their page channel and start
promoting cryptocurrency services or cover electoral news events? And, if they
do, do their existing subscribers not notice? We explore this problem of
\textit{repurposed channels}, whereby a channel changes its identity and
contents. We first characterize a market for ``second-hand'' social media
accounts, which recorded sales exceeding USD~1M during our 6-month observation
period. By observing YouTube channels (re)sold over these 6~months, we find
that a substantial number (37\%) are used to disseminate potentially harmful
content, often without facing any penalty. Even more surprisingly, these
channels seem to gain rather than lose subscribers. To estimate the prevalence
of channel repurposing ``in the wild,'' we also collect two snapshots of 1.4M
quasi-randomly sampled YouTube accounts. In a 3-month period, we estimate that
$\sim$0.25\% channels -- collectively holding $\sim$44M subscribers -- were
repurposed. We confirm that these repurposed channels share several
characteristics with sold channels -- mainly, the fact that they had a
significantly high presence of potentially problematic content. Across
repurposed channels, we find channels that became disinformation channels, as
well as channels that link to web pages with financial scams. We reason that
abusing the residual trust placed on these channels is advantageous to
financially- and ideologically-motivated adversaries. This phenomenon is not
exclusive to YouTube and we posit that the market for cultivating organic
audiences is set to grow, particularly if it remains unchallenged by
mitigations, technical or otherwise.

</details>


### [338] [Disability Across Cultures: A Human-Centered Audit of Ableism in Western and Indic LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16130)
*Mahika Phutane,Aditya Vashistha*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 西方和印度的大型语言模型在识别和评估网络残疾歧视方面存在显著差异。西方模型倾向于高估，印度模型倾向于低估。所有模型对印地语表达的残疾歧视更宽容，并受西方框架影响。印度的残疾人则从自身经历出发，更注重教育和沟通，而非简单的评判。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）虽然被用于识别和缓解网络上的仇恨言论，但现有研究多集中于西方受众和模型。本研究旨在探讨这些模型在识别印度等非西方地区的残疾歧视问题上是否足够充分，以及本地化的印度语言模型表现是否更优。

Method: 本研究采用了公开的残疾歧视言论数据集，并将其翻译成印地语。随后，研究人员提示了八个大型语言模型（四个美国开发，四个印度开发）对残疾歧视进行评分和解释。同时，研究还招募了来自美国和印度的175名残疾人来执行相同的任务。

Result: 研究结果显示，西方模型普遍高估了残疾歧视的严重程度，而印度模型则低估了其严重程度。所有模型在面对印地语表达的残疾歧视时，容忍度更高，并且倾向于采用西方的残疾歧视框架。相比之下，印度的残疾人更注重意图、人际关系和韧性，并希望通过教育来感化施害者。

Conclusion: 该研究为全球包容性残疾歧视标准奠定了基础，并强调在设计和评估人工智能系统时，必须将当地残疾人经历置于中心地位。

Abstract: People with disabilities (PwD) experience disproportionately high levels of
discrimination and hate online, particularly in India, where entrenched stigma
and limited resources intensify these challenges. Large language models (LLMs)
are increasingly used to identify and mitigate online hate, yet most research
on online ableism focuses on Western audiences with Western AI models. Are
these models adequately equipped to recognize ableist harm in non-Western
places like India? Do localized, Indic language models perform better? To
investigate, we adopted and translated a publicly available ableist speech
dataset to Hindi, and prompted eight LLMs--four developed in the U.S. (GPT-4,
Gemini, Claude, Llama) and four in India (Krutrim, Nanda, Gajendra,
Airavata)--to score and explain ableism. In parallel, we recruited 175 PwD from
both the U.S. and India to perform the same task, revealing stark differences
between groups. Western LLMs consistently overestimated ableist harm, while
Indic LLMs underestimated it. Even more concerning, all LLMs were more tolerant
of ableism when it was expressed in Hindi and asserted Western framings of
ableist harm. In contrast, Indian PwD interpreted harm through intention,
relationality, and resilience--emphasizing a desire to inform and educate
perpetrators. This work provides groundwork for global, inclusive standards of
ableism, demonstrating the need to center local disability experiences in the
design and evaluation of AI systems.

</details>


### [339] [The Impact of Pseudo-Science in Financial Loans Risk Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16182)
*Bruno Scarone,Ricardo Baeza-Yates*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 机器学习在金融信贷风险预测中可能因伪科学假设和生存偏差而产生不公平，模型性能的表面提升可能掩盖实际问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究伪科学假设在金融信贷风险预测中的社会影响，以及生存偏差对贷款回报预测的干扰，旨在揭示模型性能的真相，避免因表面现象而产生的误导。

Method: 通过机器学习分析伪科学假设在金融信贷风险预测中的应用及其对社会的影响，重点关注生存偏差问题，并从准确性和社会成本两个维度评估模型。

Result: 社会最优模型在准确性方面不会带来显著损失；模型在训练过程中可能出现准确性下降但召回率和精确度提高的现象，这是一种“幻觉”，掩盖了模型遭受不公平和生存偏差日益严重的问题。

Conclusion: 该研究通过机器学习在金融信贷风险预测中应用伪科学假设，分析了其对社会的影响，并强调了生存偏差在贷款回报预测中的作用。研究结果表明，社会最优模型在准确性方面不会带来显著损失，并且在常用学习方法和数据集上得到了验证。此外，研究还揭示了模型在训练过程中出现的自然动态：准确性略有下降，而召回率和精确度随时间提高，这可能导致观察者产生系统正在改进的错觉，但实际上模型正遭受日益严重的不公平和生存偏差。

Abstract: We study the societal impact of pseudo-scientific assumptions for predicting
the behavior of people in a straightforward application of machine learning to
risk prediction in financial lending. This use case also exemplifies the impact
of survival bias in loan return prediction. We analyze the models in terms of
their accuracy and social cost, showing that the socially optimal model may not
imply a significant accuracy loss for this downstream task. Our results are
verified for commonly used learning methods and datasets. Our findings also
show that there is a natural dynamic when training models that suffer survival
bias where accuracy slightly deteriorates, and whose recall and precision
improves with time. These results act as an illusion, leading the observer to
believe that the system is getting better, when in fact the model is suffering
from increasingly more unfairness and survival bias.

</details>


### [340] [Characterizing Online Activities Contributing to Suicide Mortality among Youth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16185)
*Aparna Ananthasubramaniam,Elyse J. Thulin,Viktoryia Kalesnikava,Silas Falde,Jonathan Kertawidjaja,Lily Johns,Alejandro Rodríguez-Putnam,Emma Spring,Kara Zivin,Briana Mezuk*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析死亡调查摘要，识别了 12 种与青少年自杀相关的在线活动，并开发了一个计算框架来模拟这些活动。研究发现这些活动与自杀风险阶段相关，并在一_定程度上受到死亡特征和 COVID-19 封锁的影响，这为开发新的干预措施提供了思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 青少年自杀率的上升凸显了理解在线体验如何加剧这一公共卫生问题的紧迫性。

Method: 本研究采用混合方法，首先对 2013-2022 年间的 29,124 份死亡调查开放文本摘要进行主题分析，识别出 12 种与青少年自杀相关的在线活动。然后，开发了一个零样本学习框架来大规模模拟这些主题，并分析了这些主题随时间以及与死亡特征（如年龄、死亡方式和人际关系问题）的变化情况。

Result: 研究识别了 12 种与自杀风险相关的在线活动，包括与自我伤害、伤害他人、人际互动、在线活动水平和生活事件相关的活动。这些活动与两种主要的自杀理论中的自杀风险不同阶段相对应。研究发现，这些主题与死亡特征相关，并在 2020 年 COVID-19 封锁期间更为普遍。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了在线活动与青少年自杀风险之间的关联，并提出了一个计算框架，可以识别与不同自杀风险阶段相关的在线活动。研究结果表明，这些在线活动在不同死亡特征之间存在差异，并且在 2020 年 COVID-19 封锁期间变得更加普遍。该研究强调了结合自杀理论和计算研究来开发针对不那么明显的自杀风险指标的干预措施的潜力。

Abstract: The recent rise in youth suicide highlights the urgent need to understand how
online experiences contribute to this public health issue. Our mixed-methods
approach responds to this challenge by developing a set of themes focused on
risk factors for suicide mortality in online spaces among youth ages 10-24, and
a framework to model these themes at scale. Using 29,124 open text summaries of
death investigations between 2013-2022, we conducted a thematic analysis to
identify 12 types of online activities that were considered by investigators or
next of kin to be relevant in contextualizing a given suicide death. We then
develop a zero-shot learning framework to model these 12 themes at scale, and
analyze variation in these themes by decedent characteristics and over time.
Our work uncovers several online activities related to harm to self, harm to
others, interpersonal interactions, activity levels online, and life events,
which correspond to different phases of suicide risk from two prominent suicide
theories. We find an association between these themes and decedent
characteristics like age, means of death, and interpersonal problems, and many
themes became more prevalent during the 2020 COVID-19 lockdowns. While digital
spaces have taken some steps to address expressions of suicidality online, our
work illustrates the opportunities for developing interventions related to less
explicit indicators of suicide risk by combining suicide theories with
computational research.

</details>


### [341] [PRAC3 (Privacy, Reputation, Accountability, Consent, Credit, Compensation): Long Tailed Risks of Voice Actors in AI Data-Economy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16247)
*Tanusree Sharma,Yihao Zhou,Visar Berisha*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了语音合成技术对配音演员造成的风险，并提出了改进的 C3 框架（PRAC3），以应对隐私、声誉和问责等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期的大规模音频数据集（如 LibriSpeech）的建立依赖于众多贡献者，但十年后，这些贡献使配音演员面临多重风险。现有的 C3 框架（同意、署名、补偿）未能充分应对语音身份在脱离语境、作者身份和控制的情况下所产生的风险。

Method: 本文通过对 20 位专业配音演员进行深度访谈，揭示了在缺乏强制性约束的情况下，语音合成复制所带来的潜在威胁。

Result: 研究发现，配音演员的语音数据可能被用于制作色情内容、政治宣传和表情包，对其声誉造成损害。更严重的是，当他们的语音被用于金融欺诈、虚假信息传播或身份冒充诈骗等高风险场景时，会出现责任不清的问题。在这种情况下，配音演员即使在没有法律代表或工会保护的情况下，也可能面临社会和法律后果。

Conclusion: 现有的 C3 框架（同意、署名、补偿）未能充分解决与语音身份相关的风险，例如被用于色情内容、政治宣传或金融欺诈。本文提出的 PRAC3 框架（隐私、声誉、问责、同意、署名、补偿）为合成语音经济中的数据治理提供了新的视角，强调了隐私、声誉、问责、同意、署名和补偿之间的相互关联性。该框架旨在解决非自愿训练带来的隐私风险，以及脱离背景使用语音造成的声誉损害，并为人工智能数据生态系统中的问责制提出了新的设想。文章最后强调，语音作为生物识别信息和创意劳动，其治理模式需要恢复创作者的代理权，确保可追溯性，并为道德再利用建立可执行的界限。

Abstract: Early large-scale audio datasets, such as LibriSpeech, were built with
hundreds of individual contributors whose voices were instrumental in the
development of speech technologies, including audiobooks and voice assistants.
Yet, a decade later, these same contributions have exposed voice actors to a
range of risks. While existing ethical frameworks emphasize Consent, Credit,
and Compensation (C3), they do not adequately address the emergent risks
involving vocal identities that are increasingly decoupled from context,
authorship, and control. Drawing on qualitative interviews with 20 professional
voice actors, this paper reveals how the synthetic replication of voice without
enforceable constraints exposes individuals to a range of threats. Beyond
reputational harm, such as re-purposing voice data in erotic content, offensive
political messaging, and meme culture, we document concerns about
accountability breakdowns when their voice is leveraged to clone voices that
are deployed in high-stakes scenarios such as financial fraud, misinformation
campaigns, or impersonation scams. In such cases, actors face social and legal
fallout without recourse, while very few of them have a legal representative or
union protection. To make sense of these shifting dynamics, we introduce the
PRAC3 framework, an expansion of C3 that foregrounds Privacy, Reputation,
Accountability, Consent, Credit, and Compensation as interdependent pillars of
data used in the synthetic voice economy. This framework captures how privacy
risks are amplified through non-consensual training, how reputational harm
arises from decontextualized deployment, and how accountability can be
reimagined AI Data ecosystems. We argue that voice, as both a biometric
identifier and creative labor, demands governance models that restore creator
agency, ensure traceability, and establish enforceable boundaries for ethical
reuse.

</details>


### [342] [Beyond Algorethics: Addressing the Ethical and Anthropological Challenges of AI Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16430)
*Octavian M. Machidon*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 人工智能推荐系统在数字世界中无处不在，但它们也引发了关于隐私、自主性和心理健康的担忧。现有方法不足以解决这些问题，需要新的方法来确保这些系统以人为本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出人工智能驱动的推荐系统（RSs）已成为塑造数字环境和社交互动核心，但其伦理含义仍探索不足，而对隐私、自主和心理健康的担忧日益加剧。

Method: 通过分析人工智能驱动的推荐系统（RSs）带来的伦理和人类学挑战，论证了现有的伦理方法（包括算法伦理）虽然必要但最终不足以解决问题，因为RSs会将人类的复杂性还原为可量化的维度，利用用户的弱点，并优先考虑参与度而非福祉。

Result: 人工智能驱动的推荐系统（RSs）不仅反映用户偏好，还在社交媒体、娱乐平台和电子商务中积极构建个人体验。

Conclusion: 需要超越纯粹的技术解决方案，建立一个全面的以人为本的推荐系统设计框架，整合跨学科视角、监管策略和教育举措，以确保人工智能系统促进而非损害人类自主性和社会繁荣。

Abstract: In this paper, I examine the ethical and anthropological challenges posed by
AI-driven recommender systems (RSs), which have become central to shaping
digital environments and social interactions. By curating personalized content,
RSs do not merely reflect user preferences but actively construct individual
experiences across social media, entertainment platforms, and e-commerce.
Despite their ubiquity, the ethical implications of RSs remain insufficiently
explored, even as concerns over privacy, autonomy, and mental well-being
intensify. I argue that existing ethical approaches, including algorethics, the
effort to embed ethical principles into algorithmic design, are necessary but
ultimately inadequate. RSs inherently reduce human complexity to quantifiable
dimensions, exploit user vulnerabilities, and prioritize engagement over
well-being. Addressing these concerns requires moving beyond purely technical
solutions. I propose a comprehensive framework for human-centered RS design,
integrating interdisciplinary perspectives, regulatory strategies, and
educational initiatives to ensure AI systems foster rather than undermine human
autonomy and societal flourishing.
